          <span id="freeTextContainer5801136260922412904">
           What do a profligate Earl, an immortal and evil Viking priest and an ancient prophecy all have in common? The beautiful young actress Jessamy Powers. A woman with a dark secret and possibly the key to a kingdom's rise or fall.
           <br/>
           <br/>
           A kingdom in the mists is more than just a myth and London is about to find itself at the epicenter of mystery, terror, romance and the revelation t
          </span>
          <span id="freeText5801136260922412904" style="display:none">
           What do a profligate Earl, an immortal and evil Viking priest and an ancient prophecy all have in common? The beautiful young actress Jessamy Powers. A woman with a dark secret and possibly the key to a kingdom's rise or fall.
           <br/>
           <br/>
           A kingdom in the mists is more than just a myth and London is about to find itself at the epicenter of mystery, terror, romance and the revelation that legendary figures still exist. Immortal evil is as determined to destroy as immortal guardians are to protect a great legacy and a great love.
           <br/>
           <br/>
           <br/>
           Author note: Some adult sexual content
          </span>

                   <span id="freeText14123742721853808502" style="display:none">
                    Ok Book lovers!!! I am on Chapter 24 in this book and all I can say is WOW!!!! I am 75% done with the book and I am enjoying it so much that I dread the end of it. It is a very unique blend of historical romance, think 1800's England, throw in a little bit of King Arthur and the magic of Merlin and you have "Rook and Raven" Book one in The Celtic King Trilogy. It has just enough hot under the collar moments to make you wonder if the room is a little warm, and just enough magic to satisfy your reading sweet tooth for fantasy adventure. Even the animals in the story have a way of drawing you in and endearing them to the reader. Full of mystery and intrigue it is a read I believe male and female both will enjoy.

                   <span id="freeText15850730669636828147" style="display:none">
                    I didn't know what to expect when I started this book, but the description sounded intriguing.  Although Sebastian (aka Rook) has a sorted past, I found myself drawn to him as a character and rooting for him to win back Jessamy's heart.  As both Sebastian and Jessy's secrets become revealed, the reader will fall more in love with them both. This book had more twists than I was expecting and had me guessing as to what the outcome would be. I'm looking forward to the next book in this series and I can't wait to see how the story will unfold.

                   <span id="freeText6480647856899344113" style="display:none">
                    So what can I say about this book? Well for one thing it is not what you expect, whatever you expect. If youre looking for intrigue and adventure check. If youre looking for period romance check, if youre looking for fantasy and magic check, all this and still room for Vikings, witches, Arthurian legend, evil priests, oh and even the battle of Waterloo plays an important part! Certainly this is a book not lacking in story by any means. And what a great story it is, drawing you in and masterfully revealing elements bit by bit until you are left waiting to find out what happens next. So if there was one downside to this book it is that part 2 is not out yet. Come on Julie I want to know what happens next!
                   </span>
                   <a data-text-id="6480647856899344113" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">
                    ...more
                   </a>
                  </span>
                 </div>

                    indie-books

                   <span id="freeTextContainer11417789168926043177">
                    I don't usually read this type of book, but after reading it I'm wondering if I should do so more often.
                    <br/>
                    <br/>
                    It was very romantic and adventurous.
                    <br/>
                    <br/>
                    There was a lot of description, which I often shy away from. But I enjoyed it here.
                    <br/>
                    <br/>
                    How do you classify this book?
                    <br/>
                    <br/>
                    There's a lot of romance. There's UK history. There's mythology and magic. There's some horror...slasher movie moments. Quite gruesome.
                    <br/>
                    <br/>
                    There were some suspenseful moments involving terrifying weapons.
                    <br/>
                    <br/>
                    There's some great erotica moments.
                    <br/>
                    <br/>
                    There's
                   </span>
                   <span id="freeText11417789168926043177" style="display:none">
                    I don't usually read this type of book, but after reading it I'm wondering if I should do so more often.
                    <br/>
                    <br/>
                    It was very romantic and adventurous.
                    <br/>
                    <br/>
                    There was a lot of description, which I often shy away from. But I enjoyed it here.
                    <br/>
                    <br/>
                    How do you classify this book?
                    <br/>
                    <br/>
                    There's a lot of romance. There's UK history.  There's mythology and magic. There's some horror...slasher movie moments.  Quite gruesome.
                    <br/>
                    <br/>
                    There were some suspenseful moments involving terrifying weapons.
                    <br/>
                    <br/>
                    There's some great erotica moments.
                    <br/>
                    <br/>
                    There's friendship and tear-jerker family moments.
                    <br/>
                    <br/>
                    There are surprises....plot twists.
                    <br/>
                    <br/>
                    There's a guy who eats scones, which is really not that important. But I liked that part because I really like scones.
                    <br/>
                    <br/>
                    The villains in the story remind me of the type of villains from Charmed, which is good for me because I liked that show.
                    <br/>
                    <br/>
                    The book also reminds me of The Princess Bride. It's a mixture of The Princess Bride and Charmed...a more sexual version of those two.
                    <br/>
                    <br/>
                    As for the plot: A young man and woman were once in love. He left her and she had a lot anger about that. Then he returns to find her an actress.  She's very angry with him, yet she's still in love with him.   So there's a lot of sexual tension.  Angry sexual tension.
                    <br/>
                    <br/>
                    That's the romantic aspect of the story. Then there's stuff with secret kings and scary priests....a lost locket.
                    <br/>
                    <br/>
                    All kinds of fun stuff. I don't want to give too much away.
                   </span>

                    This is a compelling story. Viking and Celtic magic and legend are woven into a plot that combines them with a Regency setting, in England. The book would appeal to lovers of historical fiction or fantasy, or to readers like myself, who love a combination of history and fantasy. Historical romance fans would like it, too.                    </span>
                   <span id="freeText1900604020432549266" style="display:none">
                    This is a compelling story. Viking and Celtic magic and legend are woven into a plot that combines them with a Regency setting, in England. The book would appeal to lovers of historical fiction or fantasy, or to readers like myself, who love a combination of history and fantasy. Historical romance fans would like it, too. The romantic and racy elements are a good read. The characters are so believable and the story so engrossing that it was hard to put the book down. I can hardly wait for the next book. A very impressive debut, and one of the best books I have read for a long time.

                    I normally ignore this type of book as "chick Lit" which I do not like. However, this is much more than chick lit. I love the history inherent in the story. It's obvious that the author has done historical research and has included real historical facts in this book. The characters are developed so well that they are extremely riveting. The storyline held me until the end. I now cannot wait for the second book. I highly recommend this book! It's great entertainment.

              <div class="section">
               <div class="review" id="review_928708193" itemprop="reviews" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
                <link href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/928708193" itemprop="url"/>
                <a class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5333053-maureen-kinley" title="Maureen Kinley">
                 <img alt="Maureen Kinley" src="https://d.gr-assets.com/users/1303924911p2/5333053.jpg"/>
                </a>
                <div class="left bodycol">
                 <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
                  <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/928708193?book_show_action=true" itemprop="publishDate">
                   May 05, 2014
                  </a>
                  <a class="user" href="/user/show/5333053-maureen-kinley" title="Maureen Kinley">
                   Maureen Kinley
                  </a>
                  rated it
                  <a class=" staticStars stars_5" title="it was amazing">
                   5 of 5 stars
                  </a>
                  <span class="greyText">
                   
                  </span>
                  <a class="lightGreyText" href="/book/show/22012205-rook-and-raven" title="Kindle Edition 9780692200919">
                   review of another edition
                  </a>
                 </div>
                 <div class="reviewText stacked">
                  <span class="readable" id="reviewTextContainer928708193" style="">
                   <span id="freeTextContainer4089293497576397314">
                    Sometimes I am afraid of Historical Fiction, as it might be a little more difficult to breeze through, being all wordy and descriptive, but I am extremely happy I took on Rook and Raven. A little violence, a little sex and a little magic with characters you seem to be able to relate to, it was a fantastic read! Mystical, but really engaging! I love this authors style- looking forward to the next book in the series!
                   </span>
                  </span>
                 </div>

                    <br/>
                    Format:Kindle Edition
                    <br/>
                    This was a great book. Anyone who loves historical fiction, romance, and magic (or any combination of the three), would enjoy this book. I often felt as though I could be apart of the story. The amazing details and depth of the characters pulled me in and I had difficulty putting the book down. Kudos to Julie Harvey DelCourt for such a great book. I can not wait until the sequel.

               <script charset="utf-8" type="text/javascript">
                function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked &amp;&amp; exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&amp;name=' + shelf_name + '&amp;a=' + action + '&amp;authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('lDZArzfA0jelePT2lNZdqc55F91ozOWjmsr8PCcsnsjAbv+CnGpSklISCHoBnjmqz3BFMXfpmAjPZOSM4wZVyg==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&amp;book_id=' + book_id + '&amp;refresh=true' + '&amp;authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('HlsPzNgHokWZfQaYS/O1hSlhIgoCzuA4tFy7wSGK4fBKA7Dhc60i4G4X+hTeu9GGKGhw5h3rnZPh8qNx5aAq8g==')})
  }

           <span id="freeText11895294734366684571" style="display:none">
            I spent most of my life living around the world. I loved every adventurous minute of it. I earned a B.A. in history and an M.A. in liberal arts.  I am the ultimate, at home, Jeopardy contestant lol.
            <br/>
            <br/>
            My young son adores hats almost as much as I do and has a love of cows. His first word was "cat" and I swear the second was "moo!"
            <br/>
            <br/>
            He and I both have an undying addiction to Converse tennis shoes, the X-Files and pretty much every Meg Ryan movie.
            <br/>
            <br/>
            <br/>
            Julie
